## 2.2. Order Update Request

Update notes field for an order

| PATCH | /v1/orders/:id |
| :---- | :---- |

| { "notes": {   "key1": "value3",   "key2": "value2" }} |
| :---- |

| parameter | type | Description |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| notes | object | Key-value pair that can be used to store additional information about the entity. Maximum 15 key-value pairs, 256 characters (maximum) each. For example, "note\_key": "Beam me up Scotty”. |

Response

| {   "id": "order\_DaaS6LOUAASb7Y",   "entity": "order",   "amount": 2000,   "amount\_paid": 0,   "amount\_due": 2000,   "currency": "INR",   "receipt": null,   "offer\_id": "offer\_JGQvQtvJmVDRIA",   "offers": \[       "offer\_JGQvQtvJmVDRIA"   \],   "status": "created",   "attempts": 0,   "notes": \[\],   "created\_at": 1654776878} |
| :---- |

Response parameters

| parameter | type | Description |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| id | string | The unique identifier of the order. |
| amount | integer | The amount for which the order was created, in currency subunits. For example, for an amount of ₹295.00, enter 29500\. |
| entity | string | Name of the entity. Here, it is order. |
| amount\_paid | integer | The amount paid against the order. |
| amount\_due | integer | The amount pending against the order. |
| currency | string | ISO code for the currency in which you want to accept the payment. The default length is 3 characters. Refer to the [list of supported currencies](https://razorpay.com/docs/payments/international-payments/#supported-currencies). |
| receipt | string | Receipt number that corresponds to this order. Can have a maximum length of 40 characters and has to be unique. |
| status | string | The status of the order. Possible values: created: When you create an order it is in the created state. It stays in this state till a payment is attempted on it. attempted: An order moves from created to attempted state when a payment is first attempted on it. It remains in the attempted state till one payment associated with that order is captured. paid: After the successful capture of the payment, the order moves to the paid state. No further payment requests are permitted once the order moves to the paid state. The order stays in the paid state even if the payment associated with the order is refunded. |
| attempts | integer | The number of payment attempts, successful and failed, that have been made against this order. |
| notes | Json object | Key-value pair that can be used to store additional information about the entity. Maximum 15 key-value pairs, 256 characters (maximum) each. For example, "note\_key": "Beam me up Scotty”. |
| created\_at | integer | Indicates the Unix timestamp when this order was created. |

## 2.3. Order fetch request (under review)

Fetch all orders for a merchant

| GET | /v1/orders |
| :---- | :---- |

Curl request:

| curl \-u \[YOUR\_KEY\_ID\]:\[YOUR\_KEY\_SECRET\]\\\-X GET https://api.razorpay.com/v1/orders?count=2\&skip=1 |
| :---- |

Query parameters

| parameter | type | Possible values |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| authorized | boolean | 1 : Retrieves Orders for which payments have been authorized. Payment and order states differ. 0 : Retrieves orders for which payments have not been authorized. |
| receipt | string | Retrieves the orders that contain the provided value for receipt. |
| from | integer | Timestamp (in Unix format) from when the orders should be fetched. |
| to | integer | Timestamp (in Unix format) up till when orders are to be fetched. |
| count | integer | The number of orders to be fetched. The default value is 10\. The maximum value is 100\. This can be used for pagination, in combination with skip. |
| skip | integer | The number of orders to be skipped. The default value is 0\. This can be used for pagination, in combination with count. |
| expand\[\] | array | Used to retrieve additional information about the payment. Using this parameter will cause a sub-entity to be added to the response. Supported values are: payments: Returns a collection of all payments made for each order. payments.card: Returns the card details of each payment made for each order. transfers: Returns a collection of transfers created for each order. For more information about creating transfers using orders, refer to the Transfers section of the Route API documentation. virtual\_account: Returns the virtual account details created for each order. For more information about creating Virtual Accounts, refer to the Smart Collect API [Example 1](https://razorpay.com/docs/api/orders/fetch-all-expanded-payments/) [example 2](https://razorpay.com/docs/api/orders/fetch-all-expanded-card-payments/) |

Response

| { "entity": "collection", "count": 2, "items": \[   {     "id": "order\_EKzX2WiEWbMxmx",     "entity": "order",     "amount": 1234,     "amount\_paid": 0,     "amount\_due": 1234,     "currency": "INR",     "receipt": "Receipt No. 1",     "offer\_id": null,     "status": "created",     "attempts": 0,     "notes": \[\],     "created\_at": 1582637108   },   {     "id": "order\_EAI5nRfThga2TU",     "entity": "order",     "amount": 100,     "amount\_paid": 0,     "amount\_due": 100,     "currency": "INR",     "receipt": "Receipt No. 1",     "offer\_id": null,     "status": "created",     "attempts": 0,     "notes": \[\],     "created\_at": 1580300731   } \]} |
| :---- |

Response parameters

| parameter | type | Description |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| id | string | The unique identifier of the order. |
| amount | integer | The amount for which the order was created, in currency subunits. For example, for an amount of ₹295.00, enter 29500\. |
| entity | string | Name of the entity. Here, it is order. |
| amount\_paid | integer | The amount paid against the order. |
| amount\_due | integer | The amount pending against the order. |
| currency | string | ISO code for the currency in which you want to accept the payment. The default length is 3 characters. Refer to the [list of supported currencies](https://razorpay.com/docs/payments/international-payments/#supported-currencies). |
| receipt | string | Receipt number that corresponds to this order. Can have a maximum length of 40 characters and has to be unique. |
| status | string | The status of the order. Possible values: created: When you create an order it is in the created state. It stays in this state till a payment is attempted on it. attempted: An order moves from created to attempted state when a payment is first attempted on it. It remains in the attempted state till one payment associated with that order is captured. paid: After the successful capture of the payment, the order moves to the paid state. No further payment requests are permitted once the order moves to the paid state. The order stays in the paid state even if the payment associated with the order is refunded. |
| attempts | integer | The number of payment attempts, successful and failed, that have been made against this order. |
| notes | Json object | Key-value pair that can be used to store additional information about the entity. Maximum 15 key-value pairs, 256 characters (maximum) each. For example, "note\_key": "Beam me up Scotty”. |
| created\_at | integer | Indicates the Unix timestamp when this order was created. |

## 2.5. Fetch Payments for an Order (under review)

Fetch all payments for an order

| GET | /v1/orders/:id/payments |
| :---- | :---- |

Curl request:

| curl \-u \[YOUR\_KEY\_ID\]:\[YOUR\_KEY\_SECRET\]\\\-X GET https://api.razorpay.com/v1/orders/order\_DaaS6LOUAASb7Y/payments |
| :---- |

Path parameters

| parameter | type | Description |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| id | string | Unique identifier of the order for which the payments should be retrieved. |

Response

| { "entity":"collection", "count":2, "items":\[   {     "id":"pay\_N8FUmetkCE2hZP",     "entity":"payment",     "amount":100,     "currency":"INR",     "status":"failed",     "order\_id":"order\_N8FRN5zTm5S3wx",     "invoice\_id":null,     "international":false,     "method":"upi",     "amount\_refunded":0,     "refund\_status":null,     "captured":false,     "description":null,     "card\_id":null,     "bank":null,     "wallet":null,     "vpa":"failure@razorpay",     "email":"void@razorpay.com",     "contact":"+919999999999",     "notes":{       "notes\_key\_1":"Tea, Earl Grey, Hot",       "notes\_key\_2":"Tea, Earl Grey... decaf."     },     "fee":null,     "tax":null,     "error\_code":"BAD\_REQUEST\_ERROR",     "error\_description":"Payment was unsuccessful due to a temporary issue. If amount got deducted, it will be refunded within 5-7 working days.",     "error\_source":"gateway",     "error\_step":"payment\_response",     "error\_reason":"payment\_failed",     "acquirer\_data":{       "rrn":null     },     "created\_at":1701688684,     "upi":{       "vpa":"failure@razorpay"     }   },   {     "id":"pay\_N8FVRD1DzYzBh1",     "entity":"payment",     "amount":100,     "currency":"INR",     "status":"captured",     "order\_id":"order\_N8FRN5zTm5S3wx",     "invoice\_id":null,     "international":false,     "method":"upi",     "amount\_refunded":0,     "refund\_status":null,     "captured":true,     "description":null,     "card\_id":null,     "bank":null,     "wallet":null,     "vpa":"success@razorpay",     "email":"void@razorpay.com",     "contact":"+919999999999",     "notes":{       "notes\_key\_1":"Tea, Earl Grey, Hot",       "notes\_key\_2":"Tea, Earl Grey... decaf."     },     "fee":2,     "tax":0,     "error\_code":null,     "error\_description":null,     "error\_source":null,     "error\_step":null,     "error\_reason":null,     "acquirer\_data":{       "rrn":"267567962619",       "upi\_transaction\_id":"F5B66C7C07CA6FEAD77E956DC2FC7ABE"     },     "created\_at":1701688721,     "upi":{       "vpa":"success@razorpay"     }   } \]} |
| :---- |

Response parameters

| parameter | type | Description |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| id | string | The unique identifier of the order. |
| entity | string | Indicates the type of entity. |
| amount | integer | The payment amount in currency subunits. For example, for an amount of ₹1.00 enter 100\. |
| currency | string | The currency in which the payment is made. |
| status | string | The status of the payment. Possible values: created authorized captured refunded failed |
| method | string | The payment method used for making the payment. Possible values: card netbanking wallet upi emi |
| order\_id | string | Order id, if provided. Know more about [Orders](https://razorpay.com/docs/payments/orders/). |
| description | string | Description of the payment, if any. |
| international | boolean | Indicates whether the payment is done via an international card or a domestic one. |
| refund\_status | string | The refund status of the payment. Possible values: null partial full |
| amount\_refunded | integer | The amount refunded in currency subunits. For example, if amount\_refunded \= 100, it is equal to ₹1.00. |
| captured | boolean | Indicates if the payment is captured. |
| email | string | Customer email address used for the payment. |
| contact | string | Customer contact number used for the payment. |
| fee | integer | Fee (including tax) charged by us. |
| tax | integer | Tax charged for the payment. |
| error\_code | string | Error that occurred during payment. For example, BAD\_REQUEST\_ERROR. |
| error\_description | string | Description of the error that occurred during payment. For example, Payment processing failed because of incorrect OTP. |
| error\_source | string | The point of failure. For example, customer. |
| error\_step | string | The stage where the transaction failure occurred. The stages can vary depending on the payment method used to complete the transaction. For example, payment\_authentication. |
| error\_reason | string | The exact reason for the error reason. For example, incorrect\_otp. |
| notes | json object | Contains user-defined fields, stored for reference purposes. |
| created\_at | integer | Timestamp, in UNIX format, on which the payment was created. |
| card\_id | string | The unique identifier of the card used by the customer to make the payment. |
| wallet | string | The name of the wallet used by the customer to make the payment. For example, payzapp. |
| acquirer\_data | array | A dynamic array consisting of unique reference numbers. |
| acquirer\_data.rrn | string | A unique bank reference number provided by the banking partner when a refund is processed. This reference number can be used by the customer to track the status of the refund with the bank. |
| acquirer\_data.authentication\_reference\_number | string | A unique reference number generated for RuPay card payments. |
| acquirer\_data.bank\_transaction\_id | string | A unique reference number provided by the banking partner in case of netbanking payments. |
| bank | string | The 4-character bank code which the customer's account is associated with. For example, UTIB for Axis Bank. |
| upi | object | Details of the UPI payment received. Applicable if method is upi. |
| upi.payer\_account\_type | string | The payment method used for making the payment. Possible values: bank\_account credit\_card wallet |
| upi.vpa | string | The customer's VPA (Virtual Payment Address) or UPI id used to make the payment. For example, gauravkumar@exampleupi. |
| vpa | string | The customer's VPA (Virtual Payment Address) or UPI id used to make the payment. For example, gauravkumar@exampleupi. |

# 3\. Payment API suite

The Payment Create API is a server-to-server (S2S) tool that allows merchants to send detailed payment information directly to Razorpay. This API ensures that all the necessary details about a payment are provided before processing begins, enabling smooth and efficient transactions. It includes key information such as the payment amount, currency, customer details, and any other relevant data needed to complete the payment process. By using this API, merchants can ensure accurate and secure payment handling, leading to a better experience for both the business and its customers.  
The Payment API supports various use cases, each with its own public documentation.

## 3.1. Payment Create

### 3.1.1. Request

| POST | /payments/create/json |
| :---- | :---- |

### 3.1.2. Specific Objects & Use Cases

Below are specific object code samples along with their respective use cases. This table includes the object structures, descriptions of their functionalities, and examples of how they are utilised in different scenarios. Each entry provides insight into the purpose of the object, helping developers and product managers understand how to implement them effectively.  
*Note: Example values provided in  Green colour.*  
Scroll sideways to view the full table

| Object | Structure | Use Case | Guidance on usage |
| ----- | ----- | ----- | ----- |
| validate\_payment | "validate\_payment": {       "afa\_required": "boolean"   } | Used for MHQ payments \- internal field set by MHQ **Afa required:** additional factor authentication, if set true, OTP has to be entered before payment authorization | Public |
| aadhaar | "aadhaar": {   "number": "123456789012",   "fingerprint": "fingerprint\_example",   "session\_key": "session\_key\_example",   "hmac": "hmac\_example",   "cert\_expiry": "20240101" }, | **Aadhaar Details**: This object contains the Aadhaar number and associated details for AEPS (Aadhaar Enabled Payment System) transactions.It is used to validate identity using Aadhaar data, ensuring secure and authenticated transactions. | Do not use |
| card | "card": {   "number": 1234567812345678,   "expiry\_month": 12,   "expiry\_year": 2028,   "cvv": 123,   "name": "Gaurav Kumar",   "vault": "rzpvault",   "International": null,   "is\_cvv\_optional": false,   "is\_tokenized\_card": true,   "tokenised": true,   "cryptogram\_value": "cryptogram\_value\_example",   "token\_provider": "visa",   "token\_expiry\_month": 12,   "token\_expiry\_year": 2028,   "token": "token\_example",   "provider\_type": "network",   "service\_provider\_token\_data": {},   "is\_cvv\_less": false,   "billing\_address": {} } | **Card Payment Processing**: Contains card details required for processing card payments. Ensures secure and authenticated transactions through various attributes: \-**Card Information**: Card number, expiry date, CVV, and cardholder's name.**Vault**: Specifies if the card details are stored in a vault for secure storage and future transactions.**Tokenization**: Indicates if the card is tokenized to enhance security**Cryptogram Value**: Used for verifying the card transaction.**Billing Address**: This can be used for additional verification and billing purposes. | Public |
| upi | "upi": {   "vpa": "example@upi",   "type": "collect",   "vpa\_token": "vpa\_token\_example",   "flow": "intent",   "start\_time": 1622548800,   "end\_time": 1625150400,   "provider": "provider\_example",   "expiry\_time": 60,   "payer\_account\_type": "savings" } | **UPI Payment Processing**: Contains details required for processing UPI payments. Ensures secure and authenticated transactions through various attributes.**VPA (Virtual Payment Address)**: The UPI ID used for the transaction.**Type**: Indicates the type of UPI transaction (e.g., collect).**VPA Token**: Token associated with the VPA for enhanced security.**Flow**: Describes the UPI payment flow (e.g., intent).  **Start and End Time**: Specifies the time window for the UPI transaction.**Provider**: The UPI service provider.**Expiry Time**: Time before the UPI request expires.**Payer Account Type**: Indicates the type of payer's account (e.g., savings). | Public |
| notes | "notes": {   "merchant\_order\_id": "21" } | **Order Tracking and Metadata**: Contains additional information related to the transaction. Specifically, the **merchant\_order\_id** is used to track and reference the order within the merchant’s system. This can be used for:**Order Identification**: Helps link the transaction to a specific order in the merchant’s database.**Tracking and Reporting**: Facilitates tracking of orders and generating reports for reconciliation.**Audit and Support**: Assists in auditing and customer support by providing a unique reference for the transaction. | Public |
| receiver | "receiver": {   "type": "vpa",   "id": "cust\_1AUTRUCZEW" } | **Recipient Identification**: Contains details about the recipient of the payment. Specifically, it includes: \-**Type**: Indicates the method used to identify the recipient (e.g., VPA for UPI).**ID**: Unique identifier for the recipient. This can be used for:**Payment Routing**: Directs the payment to the correct recipient based on the identifier type.**Transaction Processing**: Ensures payments are processed accurately by specifying the recipient's details.**Verification**: Helps verify and validate the recipient's information to prevent fraud. | Public |
| "bank\_account" | "bank\_account": {   "account\_number": "1234567890",   "ifsc": "HDFC0001234",   "name": "Gaurav Kumar" } | **Bank Account Collection and Validation**: Used for collecting and validating bank account details. It ensures: \-**Bank Information**: Validates the bank's IFSC code and account number to ensure correctness.**Account Verification**: Confirm that the account number matches the provided bank details.**Payment Routing** ensures payments are directed to the correct bank account, which is important for third-party validations or specific routing needs. | Public |
| "recurring\_token" | "recurring\_token": {   "notification\_id": "notification\_id\_example",   "max\_amount": 5000,   "expire\_by": 1625150400 } | **Recurring Payment Management:** This is used for managing recurring payments and subscriptions. It includes the following:**Notification ID:** This identifies the recurring payment notification for tracking and management.**Maximum Amount:** This specifies the maximum amount allowed for recurring transactions, helping in controlling payment limits.**Expiry By:** This defines the expiry timestamp for the recurring token, ensuring the token remains valid for a set period. | Public |
| “nach” | "nach": {   "signed\_form": "signed\_form\_example" } | **NACH Authorization:** Used for managing transactions that require NACH (National Automated Clearing House) authorization. It includes: **Signed Form:** Represents the NACH authorization form that has been signed by the customer, confirming their consent for the transaction. This is essential for initiating and processing NACH transactions, ensuring compliance with authorization requirements. | Public |
| “authentication” | "authentication": {   "cavv": "cavv\_example",   "cavv\_algorithm": "c",   "eci": "05",   "xid": "xid\_example",   "enrolled\_status": "Y",   "authentication\_status": "Y",   "provider\_data": {     "product\_type": "product\_type\_example",     "auth\_type": "auth\_type\_example",     "product\_transaction\_id": "product\_transaction\_id\_example",     "product\_merchant\_reference\_id": "product\_merchant\_reference\_id\_example"   } } | **Card Authentication:** Contains information for verifying the authenticity of card transactions. It ensures secure payment processing by:**CAVV and CAVV Algorithm:** Provides the Cardholder Authentication Verification Value and its algorithm for verifying the transaction's authenticity. **ECI:** Indicates the Electronic Commerce Indicator, which specifies the level of authentication used.**XID:** Represents the transaction identifier used in authentication.**Enrolled Status:** Shows whether the card is enrolled in a secure authentication program.**Authentication Status:** Indicates if the authentication was successful.**Provider Data:** Includes additional information about the product and transaction, such as product type and transaction IDs, which helps in further validation and processing. | Public |
| “browser” | "browser": {   "java\_enabled": true,   "language": "en-UK",   "javascript\_enabled": true,   "timezone\_offset": 330,   "color\_depth": 24,   "screen\_width": 30,   "screen\_height": 100 } | **Browser Information Collection:** Contains details about the user's browser environment to assist with transaction validation and user experience optimization. It is used to for**Java and JavaScript Support:** Check if Java and JavaScript are enabled, which can impact the functionality and security of web-based transactions.**Language:** Determine the language preference of the user, which can be used for localization and user interface customization**.Timezone Offset:** Helps in understanding the user's local time for transaction timing and fraud detection.**Color Depth:** Provides information about the display quality, which can assist in ensuring compatibility with web applications.**Screen Dimensions** are used to optimize the application's layout and usability based on the user's screen size. | Public |

## 3.2. Capture a payment (under review)

Initiate capture by API for a payment.

| POST | /v1/payments/:id/capture |
| :---- | :---- |

Curl request:

| curl \-u \[YOUR\_KEY\_ID\]:\[YOUR\_KEY\_SECRET\] \\\-H 'content-type: application/json' \\\-X POST https://api.razorpay.com/v1/payments/pay\_29QQoUBi66xm2f/capture \\\-d '{ "amount": 1000, "currency": "INR"}' |
| :---- |

Path parameters

| parameter | type | Description |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| id | string | Unique identifier of the payment to be retrieved. |

Request parameters

| parameter | type | Possible values |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| amount *required* | integer | The amount to be captured (should be equal to the order amount, in the smallest unit of the currency). While creating a capture request, in the amount field, enter only the amount associated with the order that is stored in your database. |
| currency *required* | String | ISO code of the currency in which the payment was made. Refer to the [list of supported currencies](https://razorpay.com/docs/payments/international-payments/#supported-currencies). |

Response  
example for upi below, other can be seen [here](https://razorpay.com/docs/api/payments/fetch-with-id/)

| { "id": "pay\_MT3PgKGazkDUUM", "entity": "payment", "amount": 1000, "currency": "INR", "status": "captured", "order\_id": "order\_MLXS6VLbhKH7i1", "invoice\_id": "inv\_MLXS5jI0oFNX2a", "international": false, "method": "upi", "amount\_refunded": 0, "refund\_status": null, "captured": true, "description": "\#MLXS5jI0oFNX2a", "card\_id": null, "bank": null, "wallet": null, "vpa": "gaurav.kumar@examplebank", "email": null, "contact": "+919000090000", "notes": \[\], "fee": 24, "tax": 4, "error\_code": null, "error\_description": null, "error\_source": null, "error\_step": null, "error\_reason": null, "acquirer\_data": {     "rrn": "322398320067" }, "created\_at": 1692694191, "upi": {     "vpa": "gaurav.kumar@examplebank" }} |
| :---- |

## 3.3. Fetch a payment (under review)

Fetch a single payment entity by id

| Get | /v1/payments/:id |
| :---- | :---- |

Curl request:

| curl \-u \[YOUR\_KEY\_ID\]:\[YOUR\_KEY\_SECRET\]\-X GET https://api.razorpay.com/v1/payments/pay\_DG4ZdRK8ZnXC3k |
| :---- |

Path parameters

| parameter | type | Description |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| id | string | Unique identifier of the payment to be captured. |

[Query parameters](https://razorpay.com/docs/api/payments/fetch-with-id)

| parameter | type | Possible values |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| expand\[\] | string | Card, emi, offers, upi |

Response

| { "id": "pay\_G3P9vcIhRs3NV4", "entity": "payment", "amount": 1000, "currency": "INR", "status": "captured", "order\_id": "order\_GjCr5oKh4AVC51", "invoice\_id": null, "international": false, "method": "card", "amount\_refunded": 0, "refund\_status": null, "captured": true, "description": "Payment for Adidas shoes", "card\_id": "card\_KOdY30ajbuyOYN", "bank": null, "wallet": null, "vpa": null, "email": "gaurav.kumar@example.com", "contact": "9000090000", "customer\_id": "cust\_K6fNE0WJZWGqtN", "token\_id": "token\_KOdY$DBYQOv08n", "notes": \[\], "fee": 1, "tax": 0, "error\_code": null, "error\_description": null, "error\_source": null, "error\_step": null, "error\_reason": null, "acquirer\_data": {   "authentication\_reference\_number": "100222021120200000000742753928" }, "created\_at": 1605871409} |
| :---- |

Sample response 1 with expand\[\]=card [here](https://razorpay.com/docs/api/payments/fetch-payment-expanded-card/)  
Sample response 2 with expand\[\]=emi [here](https://razorpay.com/docs/api/payments/fetch-payment-expanded-emi/)  
Sample response 3 with expand\[\]=offers [here](https://razorpay.com/docs/api/payments/fetch-payment-expanded-offers/)  
Sample response 4 with expand\[\]=upi [here](https://razorpay.com/docs/api/payments/fetch-payment-expanded-upi/)  
Response parameters

| parameter | type | Description |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| id | string | Unique identifier of the payment. |
| entity | string | Indicates the type of entity. |
| amount | integer | The payment amount in currency subunits. For example, for an amount of ₹1.00 enter 100\. |
| currency | string | The currency in which the payment is made. Refer to the list of [international currencies](https://razorpay.com/docs/payments/international-payments/#supported-currencies) that we support. |
| status | string | The status of the payment. Possible values: created authorized captured refunded failed |
| method | string | The payment method used for making the payment. Possible values: card netbanking wallet emi upi |
| order\_id | string | Order id, if provided. Know more about [Orders](https://razorpay.com/docs/payments/orders/). |
| description | string | Description of the payment, if any. |
| international | boolean | Indicates whether the payment is done via an international card or a domestic one. |
| refund\_status | string | The refund status of the payment. Possible values: null partial full |
| amount\_refunded | integer | The amount refunded in currency subunits. For example, if amount\_refunded \= 100, it is equal to ₹1.00. |
| captured | boolean | Indicates if the payment is captured. |
| email | string | Customer email address used for the payment. |
| contact | string | Customer contact number used for the payment. |
| fee | integer | Fee (including GST) charged by Razorpay. |
| tax | integer | GST charged for the payment. |
| error\_code | string | Error that occurred during payment. For example, BAD\_REQUEST\_ERROR. |
| error\_description | string | Description of the error that occurred during payment. For example, Payment processing failed because of incorrect OTP. |
| error\_source | string | The point of failure. For example, customer. |
| error\_step | string | The stage where the transaction failure occurred. The stages can vary depending on the payment method used to complete the transaction. For example, payment\_authentication. |
| error\_reason | string | The exact reason for the error. For example, incorrect\_otp. |
| notes | Json object | Contains user-defined fields, stored for reference purposes. |
| created\_at | integer | Timestamp, in UNIX format, on which the payment was created. |
| card\_id | string | The unique identifier of the card used by the customer to make the payment. |
| card | object | Details of the card used to make the payment. |
| card.id | string | The unique identifier of the card used by the customer to make the payment. |
| card.entity | string | The name of the entity. Here, it is card. |
| card.name | string | Name of the cardholder. |
| card.last4 | integer | The last 4 digits of the card number. |
| card.network | string | The card network. Possible values: American Express Diners Club Maestro MasterCard RuPay Unknown Visa |
| card.type | string | The card type. Possible values: credit debit prepaid unknown |
| card.issuer | string | The card issuer. The 4-character code denotes the issuing bank. This attribute will not be set for the card issued by a foreign bank. |
| card.emi | boolean | This attribute is set to true if the card can be used for EMI payment method. |
| card,sub\_type | string | The subtype of the customer's card. Possible values: customer business Know how to accept payments made by customers using [corporate cards](https://razorpay.com/docs/payments/payment-methods/cards/corporate-cards/). |
| upi | object | Details of the UPI payment received. Only applicable if method is upi. |
| upi.payer\_account\_type | string | The payment method used for making the payment. Possible values: bank\_account credit\_card wallet |
| upi.vpa | string | The customer's VPA (Virtual Payment Address) or UPI id is used to make the payment. For example, gauravkumar@exampleupi. |
| upi.flow | string | The type of UPI flow. Possible value “in\_app”. The field flow is present only in the case of Turbo UPI Payments. |
| bank | string | The 4-character bank code which the customer's account is associated with. For example, UTIB for Axis Bank. |
| vpa | string | The customer's VPA (Virtual Payment Address) or UPI id is used to make the payment. For example, gauravkumar@exampleupi. |
| wallet | string | The name of the wallet used by the customer to make the payment. For example, payzapp. |
| acquirer\_data | array | A dynamic array consisting of unique reference numbers. |
| acquirer\_data.rrn | string | A unique bank reference number provided by the banking partner when a refund is processed. This reference number can be used by the customer to track the status of the refund with the bank. |
| acquirer\_data.authentication\_reference\_number | string | A unique reference number generated for RuPay card payments. |
| acquirer\_data. bank\_transaction\_id | string | A unique reference number provided by the banking partner in case of netbanking payments. |

## 3.4. Fetch All Payments (under review)

Fetch all payments for a mechant.

| GET | /v1/payments |
| :---- | :---- |

Curl request:

| curl \-u \[YOUR\_KEY\_ID\]:\[YOUR\_KEY\_SECRET\]\-X GET https://api.razorpay.com/v1/payments?from=1593320020\&to=1624856020\&count=2\&skip=1 |
| :---- |

Query parameters

| parameter | type | Possible values |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| from | integer | UNIX timestamp, in seconds, from when payments are to be fetched. |
| to | integer | Timestamp (in Unix format) up till when payments are to be fetched. |
| count | integer | Number of payments to be fetched. Default value is 10\. Maximum value is 100\. This can be used for pagination, in combination with the skip parameter. |
| skip | integer | Number of records to be skipped while fetching the payments. |
| expand\[\] | array | Used to retrieve additional information about the payment, the method used to make the payment. The response will include a sub-entity if this parameter is used. Possible values: card: Expanded card details, usable for card and EMI payments. emi: Expanded EMI plan details, usable for EMI payments |

Response

| { "entity": "collection", "count": 2, "items": \[   {     "id": "pay\_KbCFyQ0t9Lmi1n",     "entity": "payment",     "amount": 1000,     "currency": "INR",     "status": "authorized",     "order\_id": null,     "invoice\_id": null,     "international": false,     "method": "netbanking",     "amount\_refunded": 0,     "refund\_status": null,     "captured": false,     "description": "Test Transaction",     "card\_id": null,     "bank": "IBKL",     "wallet": null,     "vpa": null,     "email": "gaurav.kumar@gmail.com",     "contact": "+919000090000",     "notes": {       "address": "Razorpay Corporate Office"     },     "fee": null,     "tax": null,     "error\_code": null,     "error\_description": null,     "error\_source": null,     "error\_step": null,     "error\_reason": null,     "acquirer\_data": {       "bank\_transaction\_id": "5733649"     },     "created\_at": 1667397881   },   {     "id": "pay\_KbCEDHh1IrU4RJ",     "entity": "payment",     "amount": 1000,     "currency": "INR",     "status": "authorized",     "order\_id": null,     "invoice\_id": null,     "international": false,     "method": "upi",     "amount\_refunded": 0,     "refund\_status": null,     "captured": false,     "description": "Test Transaction",     "card\_id": null,     "bank": null,     "wallet": null,     "vpa": "gaurav.kumar@okhdfcbank",     "email": "gaurav.kumar@gmail.com",     "contact": "+919000090000",     "notes": {       "address": "Razorpay Corporate Office"     },     "fee": null,     "tax": null,     "error\_code": null,     "error\_description": null,     "error\_source": null,     "error\_step": null,     "error\_reason": null,     "acquirer\_data": {       "rrn": "230901495295",       "upi\_transaction\_id": "6935B87A72C2A7BC83FA927AA264AD53"     },     "created\_at": 1667397781   } \]} |
| :---- |

Sample response 1 with expand\[\]=card [here](https://razorpay.com/docs/api/payments/fetch-all-payments-with-expanded-card-details/)

| card,sub\_type | string | The sub-type of the customer's card. Possible values: customer business Know how to accept payments made by customers using [corporate cards](https://razorpay.com/docs/payments/payment-methods/cards/corporate-cards/). |
| upi | object | Details of the UPI payment received. Only applicable if method is upi. |

## 3.7. Update a Payment (under review)

Updates the payment entity.

| PATCH | /v1/payments/:id |
| :---- | :---- |

Curl request:

| curl \-u \[YOUR\_KEY\_ID\]:\[YOUR\_KEY\_SECRET\]\-X PATCH https://api.razorpay.com/v1/payments/pay\_CBYy6tLmJTzn3Q/\-d '{        "notes": {                "key1": "value1",                "key2": "value2"        }}' |
| :---- |

Path parameters

| parameter | type | Description |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| id | string | Unique identifier of the payment for which the Notes field should be updated. |

| parameter | type | Possible values |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| notes | Json object | Contains user-defined fields and is stored for reference purposes. Know more about [notes](https://razorpay.com/docs/api/entity-metadata/#notes). |

| card | object | Details of the card used to make the payment. |
| card.id | string | The unique identifier of the card used by the customer to make the payment. |
| card.entity | string | The name of the entity. Here, it is card. |
| card.name | string | Name of the cardholder. |
| card.last4 | integer | The last 4 digits of the card number. |
| card.network | string | The card network. Possible values: American Express Diners Club Maestro MasterCard RuPay Unknown Visa |
| card.type | string | The card type. Possible values: credit debit prepaid unknown |
| card.issuer | string | The card issuer. The 4-character code denotes the issuing bank. This attribute will not be set for the card issued by a foreign bank. |
| card.emi | boolean | This attribute is set to true if the card can be used for EMI payment method. |
| card,sub\_type | string | The sub-type of the customer's card. Possible values: customer business Know how to accept payments made by customers using [corporate cards](https://razorpay.com/docs/payments/payment-methods/cards/corporate-cards/). |
| upi | object | Details of the UPI payment received. Only applicable if method is upi. |
| upi.payer\_account\_type | string | The payment method used for making the payment. Possible values: bank\_account credit\_card wallet |
| upi.vpa | string | The customer's VPA (Virtual Payment Address) or UPI id used to make the payment. For example, gauravkumar@exampleupi. |
| upi.flow | string | The type of UPI flow. Possible value “in\_app”. The field flow is present only in the case of Turbo UPI Payments. |
| bank | string | The 4-character bank code which the customer's account is associated with. For example, UTIB for Axis Bank. |
| vpa | string | The customer's VPA (Virtual Payment Address) or UPI id used to make the payment. For example, gauravkumar@exampleupi. |
| wallet | string | The name of the wallet used by the customer to make the payment. For example, payzapp. |
| acquirer\_data | array | A dynamic array consisting of a unique reference numbers. |
| acquirer\_data.rrn | string | A unique bank reference number provided by the banking partner when a refund is processed. This reference number can be used by the customer to track the status of the refund with the bank. |
| acquirer\_data.authentication\_reference\_number | string | A unique reference number generated for RuPay card payments. |
| acquirer\_data. bank\_transaction\_id | string | A unique reference number provided by the banking partner in case of netbanking payments. |

Customer Entity  
Customer Entity

| Version | 1.0 (Jul 23, 2024\) |
| :---- | :---- |
| Author | Aditya Singh |

# 1\. Introduction

This document serves the following purposes:

* Provide a details view into what the “customer” entity and “customer\_details” object of Orders Create request  
* Provide a comparison and overlap view of both the payloads

The "customer\_details" object is part of orders payload used for cases like RTO protection, chargeback protection etc and **does not** create/modify the customer entity (documented [here](https://razorpay.com/docs/api/customers/create/) in the public docs). The object gets stored as a blob in the "order\_meta" table of PG router service and is then consumed by respective teams as per the use case.[\[aa\]](https://docs.google.com/document/d/1vufulBF4-LYNJCixZTKtiwy4UZcqO3zcE9-hNl0iwY4/mobilebasic#cmnt27)[\[ab\]](https://docs.google.com/document/d/1vufulBF4-LYNJCixZTKtiwy4UZcqO3zcE9-hNl0iwY4/mobilebasic#cmnt28)  
Each of these scenarios making use of "customer\_details" object documents it on their respective pages as per their requirements (Example [here](https://razorpay.com/docs/payments/magic-checkout/rto-intelligence/#step-1-create-an-order) and [here](https://razorpay.com/docs/payments/payment-gateway/s2s-integration/json/v2/build-integration/international-cards/travel/#12-create-order-and-payment)).

# **2\. Customer entity (public [docs](https://razorpay.com/docs/api/customers/create/)**)

| { "id" : "cust\_1Aa00000000004", "entity": "customer", "name" : "Gaurav Kumar", "email" : "gaurav.kumar@example.com", "contact" : "9123456780", "gstin": null, "notes": {   "notes\_key\_1":"Tea, Earl Grey, Hot",   "notes\_key\_2":"Tea, Earl Grey... decaf." }, "created\_at ": 1234567890} |
| :---- |

## 2.1. Params:

| Field | Type | Description |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| **id** | string | Unique identifier of the customer. For example, cust\_1Aa00000000004. |
| **entity** | string | Indicates the type of entity. |
| **name** | string | Customer's name. Alphanumeric value with period (.), apostrophe ('), forward slash (/), at (@) and parentheses are allowed. The name must be between 3-50 characters in length. For example, Gaurav Kumar. |
| **email** | string | The customer's email address. Maximum length allowed is 64 characters. For example, gaurav.kumar@example.com. |
| **contact** | string | The customer's phone number. Maximum length allowed is 15 characters including country code. For example, \+919876543210. |
| **gstin** | string | The customer's phone number. Maximum length allowed is 15 characters including country code. For example, \+919876543210. |
| **notes** | object | The notes object can be used to store additional information about the entity. It can hold a maximum of 15 key-value pairs, 256 characters (maximum) each. For example, "note\_key": "Beam me up Scotty”. |
| **created\_at** | integer | UNIX timestamp, when the customer was created. For example, 1234567890\. |

# 3\. “Customer\_details” object

| "customer\_details": {       "name": "string",       "email": "string",       "contact": "string",       "insights": {           "order\_count": "string",           "chargeback\_count": "string",           "booking\_channel": "string",           "has\_account": "boolean",           "registered\_at": "int64",           "tier": "string"       },       "shipping\_address": {           "line1": "string",           "line2": "string",           "city": "string",           "country": "string",           "state": "string",           "zipcode": "string",           "latitude": "string",           "longitude": "string",           "name": "string",           "contact": "string",           "landmark": "string",           "tag": "string"       },       "billing\_address": {           "line1": "string",           "line2": "string",           "city": "string",           "country": "string",           "state": "string",           "zipcode": "string",           "latitude": "string",           "longitude": "string",           "name": "string",           "contact": "string",           "landmark": "string",           "tag": "string"       },       "identity": \[           {               "type": "string",               "id": "string"           }       \]   } |
| :---- |

## 3.1. Params

| Field | Type | Description |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| **name** | string | Customer's name. Alphanumeric values with period (.), apostrophe (') and parentheses are allowed. The name must be between 3-50 characters in length. For example, Gaurav Kumar |
| **contact** | string | The customer's phone number. Maximum length of 15 characters, including the country code. For example, \+919000090000. |
| **email** | string | The customer's email address. Maximum length of 64 characters. For example, gaurav.kumar@example.com. |
| **insights** | object | Additional details of the customer, including past transaction data. |
| **insights.order\_count** | integer | Total orders placed by the account so far on the merchant platform. For example, 22\. |
| **insights.chargeback\_count** | integer | Total chargeback received for the customer account on the merchant platform. For example, 4\. |
| **insights.tier** | string | Merchant’s passenger classification, such as with a frequent flyer program. In this case, you might use values such as: standard gold platinum |
| **insights.booking\_channel** | string | To share if the user is an agent, corporate, or individual. Possible values: agent corporate individual |
| **insights.has\_account** | boolean |  To denote if the buyer is on guest checkout or has logged into the account. Possible values: true: If the user is logged into the account. false: If the user is on guest checkout. |
| **insights.registered\_at** | integer | UNIX timestamp when the customer account was created with the business. For example, 1234567890\. |
| **shipping\_address** | object | Details of the customer's shipping address. |
| **shipping\_address.name** | string | The customer's name. |
| **shipping\_address.line1** | string | The first line of the customer's address. |
| **shipping\_address.line2** | string | The second line of the customer's address. |
| **shipping\_address.zipcode** | string | The customer's ZIP code. |
| **shipping\_address.contact** | string | The customer's email address. Maximum length of 64 characters. For example, gaurav.kumar@example.com. |
| **shipping\_address.city** | string | The name of the city. For example, Bengaluru. |
| **shipping\_address.state** | string | The name of the state. For example, Karnataka. |
| **shipping\_address.country** | string | ISO 3 country code of the shipping address. For example, IND. |
| **shipping\_address.tag** | string | Address tags are additional short descriptors commonly used for filtering and searching. Maximum length of 40 characters. For example, Home, Office, and so on. |
| **shipping\_address.landmark** | string | Nearest landmark to the delivery address. |
| **billing\_address** | object | Details of the customer's billing address. |
| **billing\_address.name** | string | The customer's name. |
| **billing\_address.line1** | string | The first line of the customer's address. |
| **billing\_address.line2** | string | The second line of the customer's address. |
| **billing\_address.zipcode** | string | The customer's ZIP code. |
| **billing\_address.contact** | string | The customer's email address. Maximum length of 64 characters. For example, gaurav.kumar@example.com. |
| **billing\_address.city** | string | The name of the city. For example, Bengaluru. |
| **billing\_address.state** | string | The name of the state. For example, Karnataka. |
| **billing\_address.country** | string | ISO 3 country code of the shipping address. For example, IND. |
| **billing\_address.tag** | string | Address tags are additional short descriptors commonly used for filtering and searching. Maximum length of 40 characters. For example, Home, Office, and so on. |
| **billing\_address.landmark** | string | Nearest landmark to the delivery address. |
| **identity** | object | The customer's phone number. Maximum length of 15 characters, including the country code. For example, \+919000090000. |
| **identity.type** | string | Descriptor of the identity doc type. For example, “Pan card”. |
| **identity.id** | string | Identity doc identifier For example, ABCDE1234F. |
